<style>
 /* Style Definitions */
 table.MsoNormalTable
	{mso-style-name:"Table Normal";
	mso-tstyle-rowband-size:0;
	mso-tstyle-colband-size:0;

<p class=MsoToc1><!--[if supportFields]><span lang=DE-CH><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><a name="_Toc125450873"><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:
minor-latin;mso-fareast-font-family:"MS Mincho";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-theme-font:
minor-bidi;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:DE-CH'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></a></p>

<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:11.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:"Calibri",sans-serif;mso-ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;
mso-fareast-font-family:"MS Mincho";mso-fareast-theme-font:minor-fareast;
mso-hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-theme-font:
minor-bidi;color:black;mso-themecolor:text1;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
DE-CH;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br clear=all style='page-break-before:always'>
</span><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc125450873'></span></b>

<h1 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Hlk215311829"></a><a name="_Toc215416350"></a><a
name="_Hlk215327047"><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc215416350'><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk215311829'><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Literature
Review</span></span></span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc215416350'><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk215311829'><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>: Why
Academic Work Should Be Published as HTML — and Why the Web Was Built for It</span></span></span><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk215311829'><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></span></h1>

<span style='mso-bookmark:_Hlk215311829'></span>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Academic communication has traditionally relied on formats like PDF and
print, but a strong case is emerging for publishing scholarly work as HTML on
the World Wide Web. The web itself was originally conceived as a solution for
researchers to share information freely and easily through interconnected
hypertext documents. Tim Berners-Lee (1989) proposed a universal, linked
information system for the scientific community, establishing the conceptual
foundation of the Web. He later articulated a defining principle of this
vision: “<i>The power of the Web is in its universality. Access by everyone
regardless of disability is an essential aspect</i>” </span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION
{&quot;citationID&quot;:&quot;XCR2MUPU&quot;,&quot;properties&quot;:{&quot;formattedCitation&quot;:&quot;(WAI,
2024)&quot;,&quot;plainCitation&quot;:&quot;(WAI, 2024)&quot;,&quot;noteIndex&quot;:0},&quot;citationItems&quot;:[{&quot;id&quot;:922,&quot;uris&quot;:[&quot;http://zotero.org/users/local/lQlIqKZ4/items/89K4PEWI&quot;],&quot;itemData&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:922,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;report&quot;,&quot;abstract&quot;:&quot;Accessibility
resources free online from the international standards organization: W3C Web
Accessibility Initiative
(WAI).&quot;,&quot;language&quot;:&quot;en&quot;,&quot;publisher&quot;:&quot;World
Wide Web Consortium (W3C)&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Introduction to Web
Accessibility | Web Accessibility Initiative
(WAI)&quot;,&quot;URL&quot;:&quot;https://www.w3.org/WAI/fundamentals/accessibility-intro/&quot;,&quot;author&quot;:[{&quot;family&quot;:&quot;WAI&quot;,&quot;given&quot;:&quot;&quot;}],&quot;accessed&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2025&quot;,11,29]]},&quot;issued&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2024&quot;,3,7]]}}}],&quot;schema&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json&quot;}
<span style='mso-element:field-separator'></span></span><![endif]--><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>(WAI, 2024)</span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>. This literature review examines why the web’s
underlying design principles make HTML an ideal format for academic work.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416351"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Accessibility and Universality of Content</span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc215416351'></span><span style='mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>A core principle of the World Wide Web is
that it should work for all people, regardless of hardware, software, language,
location, or ability </span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION
{&quot;citationID&quot;:&quot;D38gjB9f&quot;,&quot;properties&quot;:{&quot;formattedCitation&quot;:&quot;(WAI,
2024)&quot;,&quot;plainCitation&quot;:&quot;(WAI, 2024)&quot;,&quot;noteIndex&quot;:0},&quot;citationItems&quot;:[{&quot;id&quot;:922,&quot;uris&quot;:[&quot;http://zotero.org/users/local/lQlIqKZ4/items/89K4PEWI&quot;],&quot;itemData&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:922,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;report&quot;,&quot;abstract&quot;:&quot;Accessibility
resources free online from the international standards organization: W3C Web
Accessibility Initiative
(WAI).&quot;,&quot;language&quot;:&quot;en&quot;,&quot;publisher&quot;:&quot;World
Wide Web Consortium (W3C)&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Introduction to Web
Accessibility | Web Accessibility Initiative
(WAI)&quot;,&quot;URL&quot;:&quot;https://www.w3.org/WAI/fundamentals/accessibility-intro/&quot;,&quot;author&quot;:[{&quot;family&quot;:&quot;WAI&quot;,&quot;given&quot;:&quot;&quot;}],&quot;accessed&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2025&quot;,11,29]]},&quot;issued&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2024&quot;,3,7]]}}}],&quot;schema&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json&quot;}
<span style='mso-element:field-separator'></span></span><![endif]--><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>(WAI, 2024)</span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>. Web accessibility standards WAI (2024) <span
class=GramE>emphasize</span> designing content so that people with disabilities
can perceive and navigate it, which in turn benefits everyone in various
contexts such as mobile-phone or low-bandwidth users. HTML is inherently suited
for accessibility because it supports semantic structure such as headings and
alt text for images that assistive technologies can interpret. Publishing
research in HTML directly aligns with these ideals: it ensures research
findings can be accessed by the widest audience, including people with disabilities
and those using diverse devices. Academic knowledge disseminated as accessible
web content thus upholds the web’s universality and the principle that the web
is “<i>for all people</i>” including those with visual, auditory, cognitive, or
motor impairments </span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION
{&quot;citationID&quot;:&quot;e37l1ZUR&quot;,&quot;properties&quot;:{&quot;formattedCitation&quot;:&quot;(W3C,
2021)&quot;,&quot;plainCitation&quot;:&quot;(W3C, 2021)&quot;,&quot;noteIndex&quot;:0},&quot;citationItems&quot;:[{&quot;id&quot;:924,&quot;uris&quot;:[&quot;http://zotero.org/users/local/lQlIqKZ4/items/KIZ2W79U&quot;],&quot;itemData&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:924,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;report&quot;,&quot;publisher&quot;:&quot;World
Wide Web Consortium (W3C)&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;W3C TAG Ethical Web
Principles&quot;,&quot;URL&quot;:&quot;https://www.w3.org/2001/tag/doc/ethical-web-principles-20210927.html&quot;,&quot;author&quot;:[{&quot;family&quot;:&quot;W3C&quot;,&quot;given&quot;:&quot;&quot;}],&quot;accessed&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2025&quot;,11,29]]},&quot;issued&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2021&quot;,9,27]]}}}],&quot;schema&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json&quot;}
<span style='mso-element:field-separator'></span></span><![endif]--><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>(W3C, 2021)</span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>.</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>
</span><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>By
contrast, academic PDFs often present barriers because text might not reflow on
small screens or images might lack alternative text, which makes them
challenging for screen readers and mobile devices.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416352"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Hypertext, Linking, and the Web’s Architecture</span></a><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc215416352'></span><span style='mso-bidi-font-family:
"Times New Roman";mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>HTML stands for <span class=SpellE>HyperText</span>
Markup Language, with hypertext being the defining feature of the web. The
web’s architecture was built around the concept of interconnected documents
identified by URLs, which allow anyone to link resources together into a “<i>remarkable
information space of interrelated resources</i>” spanning all languages and
media </span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;
mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION
{&quot;citationID&quot;:&quot;1OaDYAvO&quot;,&quot;properties&quot;:{&quot;formattedCitation&quot;:&quot;(W3C
Technical Architecture Group, 2004)&quot;,&quot;plainCitation&quot;:&quot;(W3C
Technical Architecture Group,
2004)&quot;,&quot;noteIndex&quot;:0},&quot;citationItems&quot;:[{&quot;id&quot;:926,&quot;uris&quot;:[&quot;http://zotero.org/users/local/lQlIqKZ4/items/DHAWFYZY&quot;],&quot;itemData&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:926,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;report&quot;,&quot;publisher&quot;:&quot;World
Wide Web Consortium (W3C)&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Architecture of the
World Wide Web, Volume
One&quot;,&quot;URL&quot;:&quot;https://www.w3.org/TR/webarch/&quot;,&quot;author&quot;:[{&quot;family&quot;:&quot;W3C
Technical Architecture
Group&quot;,&quot;given&quot;:&quot;&quot;}],&quot;accessed&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2025&quot;,11,29]]},&quot;issued&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2004&quot;,12,15]]}}}],&quot;schema&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json&quot;}
<span style='mso-element:field-separator'></span></span><![endif]--><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>(W3C Technical Architecture Group, 2004)</span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>. Hyperlinks are not just a technical
convenience; they are fundamental to scholarly work, where referencing and
building upon prior knowledge is key. The Architecture of the World Wide Web
notes that a format should support embedded links; otherwise it creates
dead-ends: “<i>Good practice: Hypertext links… Data formats that do not allow
content authors to create hypertext links lead to the creation of ‘terminal
nodes’ on the Web.</i>” </span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION
{&quot;citationID&quot;:&quot;J80KGDgC&quot;,&quot;properties&quot;:{&quot;formattedCitation&quot;:&quot;(W3C
Technical Architecture Group, 2004)&quot;,&quot;plainCitation&quot;:&quot;(W3C
Technical Architecture Group,
2004)&quot;,&quot;noteIndex&quot;:0},&quot;citationItems&quot;:[{&quot;id&quot;:926,&quot;uris&quot;:[&quot;http://zotero.org/users/local/lQlIqKZ4/items/DHAWFYZY&quot;],&quot;itemData&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:926,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;report&quot;,&quot;publisher&quot;:&quot;World
Wide Web Consortium (W3C)&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Architecture of the
World Wide Web, Volume
One&quot;,&quot;URL&quot;:&quot;https://www.w3.org/TR/webarch/&quot;,&quot;author&quot;:[{&quot;family&quot;:&quot;W3C
Technical Architecture
Group&quot;,&quot;given&quot;:&quot;&quot;}],&quot;accessed&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2025&quot;,11,29]]},&quot;issued&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2004&quot;,12,15]]}}}],&quot;schema&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json&quot;}
<span style='mso-element:field-separator'></span></span><![endif]--><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>(W3C Technical Architecture Group, 2004)</span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>. PDF documents, while they can contain
clickable links, are often treated as self-contained endpoints – “<i>terminal
nodes</i>” that are not seamlessly integrated into the live web of content. In
contrast, an HTML scholarly article is part of the live web: its references can
be clickable hyperlinks to sources or datasets, and it can itself be indexed,
linked to, and accessed directly via a URL. This structure supports what
Berners-Lee called a “<i>web of documents</i>” enabling researchers to connect
citations, datasets, and context in a dynamic way </span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION
{&quot;citationID&quot;:&quot;mjZ5c5js&quot;,&quot;properties&quot;:{&quot;formattedCitation&quot;:&quot;(Berners-Lee,
2006)&quot;,&quot;plainCitation&quot;:&quot;(Berners-Lee, 2006)&quot;,&quot;noteIndex&quot;:0},&quot;citationItems&quot;:[{&quot;id&quot;:940,&quot;uris&quot;:[&quot;http://zotero.org/users/local/lQlIqKZ4/items/JW8ZDAYN&quot;],&quot;itemData&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:940,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;report&quot;,&quot;publisher&quot;:&quot;World
Wide Web Consortium (W3C)&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;Linked Data - Design
Issues&quot;,&quot;URL&quot;:&quot;https://www.w3.org/DesignIssues/LinkedData&quot;,&quot;author&quot;:[{&quot;family&quot;:&quot;Berners-Lee&quot;,&quot;given&quot;:&quot;Tim&quot;}],&quot;accessed&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2025&quot;,11,29]]},&quot;issued&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2006&quot;,7,27]]}}}],&quot;schema&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json&quot;}
<span style='mso-element:field-separator'></span></span><![endif]--><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>(Berners-Lee, 2006)</span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>. Using HTML for academic work thus takes
full advantage of the web’s hypertext architecture – enabling any reader to
immediately navigate from a citation to the cited source, or from an article to
related materials, thereby enriching the research dialogue. By publishing in
HTML, academics ensure their work participates in the interconnected scholarly
conversation rather than remaining a siloed document.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416353"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Open Standards and Interoperability</span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:
_Toc215416353'></span><span style='mso-bidi-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Underpinning the success of the web is a
commitment to open standards and interoperability. HTML, CSS and JavaScript,
the core web technologies, are open and royalty-free, meaning anyone can
implement or use them </span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION
{&quot;citationID&quot;:&quot;LbKnp479&quot;,&quot;properties&quot;:{&quot;formattedCitation&quot;:&quot;(W3C,
2021)&quot;,&quot;plainCitation&quot;:&quot;(W3C, 2021)&quot;,&quot;noteIndex&quot;:0},&quot;citationItems&quot;:[{&quot;id&quot;:924,&quot;uris&quot;:[&quot;http://zotero.org/users/local/lQlIqKZ4/items/KIZ2W79U&quot;],&quot;itemData&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:924,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;report&quot;,&quot;publisher&quot;:&quot;World

EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>. The <span class=SpellE>OpenStand</span> (2012)
principles for modern standards highlight “<i>availability of standards to all</i>”
and “<i>voluntary adoption</i>”, along with transparency and consensus in their
development </span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;

EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>. In practical terms, an academic article
published as HTML adheres to an open standard that any web browser, tool, or
user can access without specialized software or paywalls. It is not locked into
a proprietary format or a single vendor’s ecosystem. Indeed, the W3C website
emphasizes that data on the Web should not be “<i>locked <span class=GramE>in
to</span> particular systems or be only readable by the applications which
created it. Users should be free to switch between applications and share data
between them</i>” a point also cited in the agency slides from <i>The Socially
Aware Web</i> course </span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='mso-ansi-language:

style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>. A PDF often requires a specific reader or
plugin and can have poor interoperability, for example because data or figures
inside PDFs cannot be easily reused or extracted. HTML content, on the other
hand, can be consumed by web browsers, indexed by search engines, repurposed
with ease, for example by converting it to other formats or text-mining it, and
remains accessible as technologies evolve. Open standards also future-proof
scholarly knowledge: well-formed HTML is likely to remain <span class=SpellE>renderable</span>
for decades thanks to the web community’s commitment to backward compatibility
and archiving, whereas obscure or proprietary formats risk obsolescence. By
publishing academic work in HTML, scholars leverage the web’s open,
interoperable foundation, ensuring their work is maximally available and
usable, embodying the idea that open access to information empowers knowledge
for all </span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416354"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>End-User Focus and Ethical Considerations</span></a><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>The literature also highlights that web
technologies and content should be designed with a user-first mindset. The
IETF’s “<i>The Internet is for End Users</i>” (RFC 8890) and W3C’s “<i>Priority
of Constituencies</i>” principle assert that when making design or publishing
decisions, the needs of end users should come before those of authors,
implementers, or platforms </span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION

of the TAG, 2025)</span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>. Applying this
ethic to academic publishing: the paramount goal is to serve the reader’s
experience and access. An HTML publication offers a reader-responsive
experience, as content can adapt to different screen sizes, users can adjust
text size or styles, and assistive technologies can better interpret structured
HTML. It also allows interactive elements such as embedded multimedia or data
visualizations that can aid understanding. These features clearly benefit the
end user. A static PDF, by contrast, often offers a one-size-fits-all layout
with fixed pagination designed for printing, which on a small screen or for a
visually impaired reader is far from ideal. Ethical web principles state, “<i>the
web should empower an equitable, informed and interconnected society</i>”
enabling knowledge-sharing for everyone </span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span

style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>. Publishing academic work as HTML directly
supports an equitable knowledge ecosystem: it makes information available to
anyone with web access, not just those with access to specific journals or
software. Scientific and scholarly information, when freely accessible on the
open web, empowers education, innovation, and informed citizenship globally. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416355"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Conclusion</span></a><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>In conclusion, the reviewed materials
collectively argue that publishing academic work as HTML is not merely a
technical choice, but a choice that upholds the very values the Web was built
upon. It maximizes accessibility and inclusion </span><!--[if supportFields]><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION

<span style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br
clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:8.0pt;line-height:107%'><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h1 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416356"></a><a name="_Hlk215327068"><span
style='mso-bookmark:_Toc215416356'><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>Reflective
Essay</span></span></a><span style='mso-bookmark:_Toc215416356'><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>: Imagining an Academic Future in HTML</span></span><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>I
still remember the first time I tried to read a dense academic PDF on my phone.
I pinched, zoomed, scrolled horizontally by accident, lost my place, and
eventually gave up. The document felt like a caged animal, alive with ideas yet
trapped inside an unyielding frame designed for A4 paper. At the time, I did not
question it. PDFs were “<i>how academia works</i>”. End of story.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Then
came <a name="_Hlk215413622"><i>The Socially Aware Web</i> course</a>—and the
story changed.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416357"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>The Course That Shifted My Perspective</span></a><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>From
the very first lecture it became clear that the Web was never meant to be a
glorified digital filing cabinet. Seeing the evolution of media from cave
paintings to the first hypertext systems made me realize something surprising:
every major leap in communication came from a shift in the medium, not just the
message. McLuhan’s “<i>medium is the message</i>” hit differently when I saw
the Web described as a <i>social machine </i></span><!--[if supportFields]><i><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US'><span style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION
{&quot;citationID&quot;:&quot;BPSHbnc8&quot;,&quot;properties&quot;:{&quot;formattedCitation&quot;:&quot;(McLuhan
et al., 1967)&quot;,&quot;plainCitation&quot;:&quot;(McLuhan et al., 1967)&quot;,&quot;noteIndex&quot;:0},&quot;citationItems&quot;:[{&quot;id&quot;:949,&quot;uris&quot;:[&quot;http://zotero.org/users/local/lQlIqKZ4/items/I3NUF2W8&quot;],&quot;itemData&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:949,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;motion_picture&quot;,&quot;abstract&quot;:&quot;Issued
in two parts; Investigates the central ideas of Marshall McLuhan using
pictorial techniques and including his own comments. Examines the reaction of
others to his views and points out that his interest is the impact of
electronic technology on the contemporary
world&quot;,&quot;dimensions&quot;:&quot;51:55&quot;,&quot;language&quot;:&quot;eng&quot;,&quot;license&quot;:&quot;This
is Marshall McLuhan: The Medium is the Message&quot;,&quot;publisher&quot;:&quot;New
York : NBC ; released by McGraw-Hill Book
Co.&quot;,&quot;source&quot;:&quot;Internet
Archive&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;This is Marshall McLuhan: The Medium is
the Message&quot;,&quot;title-short&quot;:&quot;This is Marshall
McLuhan&quot;,&quot;URL&quot;:&quot;http://archive.org/details/thisismarshallmcluhanthemediumisthemessage&quot;,&quot;director&quot;:[{&quot;family&quot;:&quot;McLuhan&quot;,&quot;given&quot;:&quot;Marshall&quot;},{&quot;literal&quot;:&quot;National
Broadcasting Company&quot;},{&quot;literal&quot;:&quot;McGraw-Hill Book
Company&quot;}],&quot;accessed&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2025&quot;,11,30]]},&quot;issued&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;1967&quot;]]}}}],&quot;schema&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json&quot;}
<span style='mso-element:field-separator'></span></span></i><![endif]--><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>(McLuhan et
al., 1967)</span><!--[if supportFields]><i><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span></i><![endif]--><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US'>. It dawned on me that academic PDFs are relics of the printing age
awkwardly transplanted into a digital environment. Meanwhile, the Web, with its
open standards and universal access, is a thriving ecosystem waiting for
academia to catch up.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416358"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>My Frustration with PDFs (and Proprietary Tools)</span></a><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>I
began thinking about my own experiences:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l17 level1 lfo54;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Downloading a 50 MB PDF
just to read a 3-page methods section.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l17 level1 lfo54;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Searching within a document
only to find that the text was <span class=GramE>actually an</span> image.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l17 level1 lfo54;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Trying to copy a paragraph
and getting broken line breaks and numbering.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l17 level1 lfo54;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Struggling to navigate
using a screen reader in a volunteer accessibility project.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Every
one of those frustrations mapped directly onto a problem the course materials
discussed: lack of interoperability, accessibility failures, and reliance on
proprietary ecosystems. PDFs freeze content in place. They privilege layout
over meaning. They enforce a visual rigidity that’s completely at odds with the
Web’s principles.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416359"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Experiencing HTML as a Living Document</span></a><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>During
the course, when I opened <i>The Socially Aware Web</i> course slides in HTML,
something clicked. They were not just <span class=GramE>slides,</span> they
were documents built to be explored. I could link to specific sections, access
embedded videos, view images with alternative text, and follow standards
references in context. HTML wasn’t a format. HTML was a space. As I explored
this idea further, I started imagining what academic life would look like if
our papers were designed in the same way, with <span class=SpellE>interaktive</span>
graphs instead of static screenshots, fine-grained annotations à la <span
class=SpellE>dokieli</span>, machine-readable metadata integrated directly into
the document, and live references that update automatically when new versions
become available </span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-begin'></span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>ADDIN ZOTERO_ITEM CSL_CITATION
{&quot;citationID&quot;:&quot;1IeirzBA&quot;,&quot;properties&quot;:{&quot;formattedCitation&quot;:&quot;(Capadisli,
n.d.)&quot;,&quot;plainCitation&quot;:&quot;(Capadisli, n.d.)&quot;,&quot;noteIndex&quot;:0},&quot;citationItems&quot;:[{&quot;id&quot;:950,&quot;uris&quot;:[&quot;http://zotero.org/users/local/lQlIqKZ4/items/FBLHLGMM&quot;],&quot;itemData&quot;:{&quot;id&quot;:950,&quot;type&quot;:&quot;report&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;dokieli&quot;,&quot;URL&quot;:&quot;https://dokie.li/&quot;,&quot;author&quot;:[{&quot;family&quot;:&quot;Capadisli&quot;,&quot;given&quot;:&quot;Sarven&quot;}],&quot;accessed&quot;:{&quot;date-parts&quot;:[[&quot;2025&quot;,11,30]]}}}],&quot;schema&quot;:&quot;https://github.com/citation-style-language/schema/raw/master/csl-citation.json&quot;}
<span style='mso-element:field-separator'></span></span><![endif]--><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US'>(Capadisli,
n.d.)</span><!--[if supportFields]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span
style='mso-element:field-end'></span></span><![endif]--><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>.
Even readers would benefit from being able to switch languages at the interface
level, thanks to built-in internationalization support. Suddenly, the idea of
submitting work as HTML did not feel like rebellion</span><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'> </span><a name="_Hlk215413240"><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US'>–</span></a><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'> it felt like realism.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416360"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Accessibility as a Moral Imperative</span></a><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>One
lecture moment stayed with me: the reminder that “<i>the Web is for all people</i>”.
That sentence took on even greater significance when I began thinking about
fictive individuals during the course. Let us imagine two students: Alex, who
has a screen reader due to a visual impairment, and Lea, who accesses the
internet via a slow connection in a rural region. Both are passionate learners,
eager to read cutting-edge research. A traditional academic article delivered
as a PDF can be a dead-end for them. It may be inaccessible, heavy to download,
or poorly structured. But an HTML version? It’s lightweight, responsive,
semantically rich. It works with Alex’s screen reader, adapting to Lea’s
device. It just works. The Web was built for these users. The W3C’s
accessibility principles are not just checklists; they are an ethos: design so
everyone can participate. In HTML, this ethos is real through alt text, proper
headings, landmarks, semantic structure, language tags, alt text, ARIA roles
and responsive layouts. When academic content is presented this way, it says:
You matter. Your access matters. <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Reflecting
on this made something crystal clear: <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><b><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>If
we choose a format that excludes people, we are responsible for the exclusion.</span></b><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:
EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Neglecting
accessibility is not a neutral act – it is an academic version of building
stairs where a ramp should be.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416361"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>The Ethical Dimension: Control, Centralization, and Agency</span></a><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>The
course delved deep into governance, centralization risks, and the erosion of
user agency. It made me realize that academic publishing’s dependence on PDFs
and proprietary platforms is not just inconvenient<a name="_Hlk215413454"> – </a>it
is political.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>When
a paper lives as a PDF:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<ul style='margin-top:0cm' type=disc>
 <li class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-bottom:5.0pt;text-align:
     justify;line-height:150%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo56;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><span
     style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;
     mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>It is locked into a single representation.<o:p></o:p></span></li>
</ul>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo56;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>It often sits behind
paywalls or platform restrictions.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo56;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Its structure is opaque to
search engines and assistive tech.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo56;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>It cannot participate fully
in linked data ecosystems.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l34 level1 lfo56;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>It reinforces power
structures in academic publishing.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>HTML,
by contrast, supports self-publishing and decentralization. It empowers scholars
to own their work, host it on their own domains, and contribute to the global
knowledge commons.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>I
found myself imagining a world where every researcher maintains a small “<i>digital
garden</i>” of their papers – interlinked, annotated, remixable, <span
class=SpellE>queryable</span>. A world where academic publishing looks less
like a warehouse and more like a vibrant ecosystem.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416362"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Imagining a Scientific Future in HTML</span></a><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Let
me paint the picture I now carry with me:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>You
publish your research on your own website as an HTML document. It includes a
live dataset, interactive visualizations, and annotations from colleagues. A
student halfway across the world reads it on their phone, perfectly rendered.
They highlight a paragraph and add a public annotation via a Web-standard
protocol.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>A
week later, someone in another country forked your dataset, added new entries,
and linked your analysis to theirs using RDF. A search engine indexes both the
document and the data structure, making it discoverable by topic and
methodology <a name="_Hlk215413552">–</a> not just keywords.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Your
work does not sit in a drawer. It lives on the Web, woven into the fabric of
global knowledge.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>This
is not science fiction. The technologies already exist. What is missing is
cultural adoption.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416363"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>From Reflection to Commitment</span></a><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>By
the end of the course, I found myself returning again and again to one idea:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Choosing
HTML is choosing the future of scholarship.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>It
is a decision grounded in:<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo57;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>accessibility<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo57;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>transparency<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo57;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>interoperability<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo57;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>ethics<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo57;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>sustainability<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo57;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>decentralization<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:35.7pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:
-17.85pt;line-height:150%;mso-list:l11 level1 lfo57;tab-stops:list 36.0pt'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:10.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:Symbol;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>durability<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>It
aligns with the Web’s design and with academic values: openness, verifiability,
and shared progress.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Publishing
as HTML no longer feels like an eccentric experiment. It feels like a
responsibility.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='mso-list:none'><a name="_Toc215416364"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Conclusion: A Personal Turning Point</span></a><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Writing
this reflection in HTML (as I intend to submit it) feels like participating,
however modestly, in that future. For the first time, my academic work is not
confined to a static page – it is living in the medium it was meant for.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>The
course gave me more than technical knowledge. It gave me a new narrative: that
the Web was built for documents like ours<a name="_Hlk215413713"> – </a>and
that academia, when it embraces this medium, becomes more inclusive, more
ethical, and more alive.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>Maybe
someday we will look back at PDFs the way we look at the printing press on <i>The
Socially Aware Web</i> course slides – an important chapter in history, but no
longer the main story.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
margin-left:0cm;text-align:justify;line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:150%;mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'>And
maybe, in that future, our scholarship will finally feel at home.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<span style='font-size:11.0pt;mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;line-height:107%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman";
mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US;mso-bidi-language:AR-SA'><br
clear=all style='mso-special-character:line-break;page-break-before:always'>
</span>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:8.0pt;line-height:107%'><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:EN-US'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

EN-US'>References</span></a><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=berschrift1ohneNumm><a name="_Toc215416367"><span style='mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>Declaration of Authorship</span></a><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default><span style='font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='text-align:justify;line-height:120%'><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>“I hereby declare, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that I have written this thesis
independently, <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that I have written the thesis using only
the aids specified in the <span class=GramE>index;</span> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that all parts of the thesis produced with
the help of aids have been <span class=GramE>declared;</span> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that I have handled both input and output
responsibly when using AI. I confirm that I have therefore only read in public
data or data released with consent and that I have checked, de-<span
class=SpellE>clared</span> and comprehensibly referenced all results and/or
other forms of AI assistance in the re-quired form and that I am aware that I
am responsible if incorrect content, violations of data protection law,
copyright law or scientific misconduct (e.g. plagiarism) have also occurred
un-intentionally; <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that I have mentioned all sources used and
cited them correctly according to established aca-demic citation <span
class=GramE>rules;</span> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that I have acquired all immaterial rights
to any materials I may have used, such as images or graphics, or that these
materials were created by <span class=GramE>me;</span> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that the topic, the thesis or parts of it
have not already been the object of any work or <span class=SpellE>examina-tion</span>
of another course, unless this has been expressly agreed with the faculty
member in ad-<span class=SpellE>vance</span> and is stated as such in the <span
class=GramE>thesis;</span> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that I am aware of the legal provisions
regarding the publication and dissemination of parts or the entire thesis and
that I comply with them <span class=GramE>accordingly;</span> <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-left:36.0pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that I am aware that my thesis can be
electronically checked for plagiarism and for third-party authorship of human
or technical origin and that I hereby grant the University of <span
class=SpellE><span class=GramE>St.Gallen</span></span> the copyright according
to the Examination Regulations as far as it is necessary for the <span
class=SpellE>administra-tive</span> actions; <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=Default style='margin-top:6.0pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:0cm;
margin-left:36.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-list:l38 level1 lfo68'><![if !supportLists]><span
style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:"Times New Roman"'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>•<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;
font-family:"Times New Roman",serif'>that I am aware that the University will
prosecute a violation of this Declaration of Authorship and that disciplinary
as well as criminal consequences may result, which may lead to expulsion from
the University or to the withdrawal of my title.” <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:8.0pt;margin-top:0cm;mso-margin-bottom-alt:
0cm;mso-margin-top-alt:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;text-align:justify;line-height:
120%'><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:11.0pt;line-height:120%;mso-ansi-language:
EN-US'>By submitting this thesis, I confirm through my conclusive action that I
am submitting the Declaration of Authorship, that I have read and understood
it, and that it is true.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:6.0pt;text-align:justify;line-height:120%'><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:DE-AT'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:6.0pt;text-align:justify;line-height:120%'><span
style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US;mso-fareast-language:DE-AT'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-ansi-language:EN-US'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
